 By doing this, your phone battery will be charged quickly

 Turn off GPS
 Also turn off GPS whenever you put the phone on charge

 Turn it on where necessary
 airplane mod kaa istemaal karenphone ko charge main lagane se pehle or jhat se bydaree charge karne kaa yah sabase behtareen tarika he
 Put the phone into airplane mode

 The unique poetic vision of Viren Dungwal was a necessary intervention in his time, identifying Vedic symbols like Parjanya, Vanya, Varuna, Dyaus and highly cosmic objects like camel, elephant, cow, fly, samosa, papaya, tamarind
 vidmbana, vyangy, prahasan or ek maanviya abrdity kaa ahsaas viren kii kavita ke jane-pahachaane kargar tatva rahe hai or ek gahari raajnneetik patibaddhta se judakar ve hashiyon par rah rahi manushyata kii aawaaj ban jate hai
 His poems have such an elaboration of poetics, which makes it possible to have more basic poetry, covering the home and the outside, private and public, internal and external
 vicitra, atpati, ashakt, dabi-kuchli or kujaat kahi jane vaali chijen yahan paraspar sanyojit hokar shakti, satta or kuleenata se ek anayas bahes chede rahati hai or ham pate hai ki choti chizon main kitna bada sangharsh or kitna bada soundarya chipa hua he
 The eloquence of humanity composed of ordinary people, animals and objects and a deep expectation of change in status quo is the main voice of Viren Dangwal's poems
 is swar ke vistaar ko, usamen halchal karte anubhavon ko dekhnaa-mahasoos karnaa hi ek romaanchak anubhav he
 Viren has never been with so much affection in Hindi poetry before Dungwal
 khaas baat yah he ki saadhaaran kii yah gaatha viren swayan bhi ek saadhaaran manushya ke, usee ke ek hisse ke rup main prastut karte hai 
 Where the state of being in the vicious circle of the shrew changes the discomfort of being in the vicious circle of man
 aaj viren dangwaal ke janmdin par unke sahitya academy puraskaar se sammanit kavy sankalan 'dushchakr main srashta' se paanch chuni hui kavitaayen
 This collection of poems by Dungwal takes us into a world with its unique name, which has become more complex and more difficult over the years and the meaning has become more restless
 1
 Our society, who does not want to be loved, who will not want to get food and clothes, who will not think that if the roof is over the head, then the treatment should be given to the little daughter, the son should be respected in the world; Do not be afraid, even if you go to the office, do not panic? Do not be confused with strangers
 kuch chintaa bhi hon, haan koi haraj nahinpar aisi nahin ki man unamem hi gale ghunehausla dilaane or barajane aasapaasho sangi-saathi, apane pyaare, khub dhane
 Papad-chutney, Aancha-pancha, Halla-gullado char jashan can also be seen, sometimes, it is possible to make some splashes, as far as this world can go, who would not want to roam around? isamen jo damak rahaa, shartiya kaala he
 He is getting murdered, innocent and gentleman at the Sarsham crossroads, who is innocent and who has created such a society
 jisamen bas vahi damakata he, jo kaala he ?motor safed vah kaali haive gaal gulabi kaale hanchintaakul, chehrabudhimanpothe kanoonee kaale hanate kii thili kaali he
 Every breath is black and black is black
 The magnificent building of black people is black
 kaalepan kii ve santaanenhain bicha raheen jin kaali ichchhaaon kii bisaatav apane kaalepan se hamako gher rahishepana kaala jaadu he ham par pher rahibolo to, kuch karnaa bhi he
 Or to die while drinking black syrup? 2
 motorcycle par sainikbatti puure ilaake kii gummai tahalta tha chhavnee kii ek pedo bhari sadak parasunil ke saathtabhi safed helmet pahana ek sainik pulicekahin se niklaur motorcycle start karne laga
 In the third time, the car started to move, it increased a bit, then turned to the shoulder and in the back groin, he touched the box of fantastin with his right hand and saw us in that moon-filled darkness
 ek rajasi ghode kii si harakat thimeh pal-bhar kaa ghurnatatolana, ndehviheen ghoorna
 Then he went to make a tunnel of light on the winding road behind the spring in the clear night, with headlight, we also saw it in the moonlight-filled darkness
 ek rajasi ghode kii aisi harakat thimeh pal-bhar-kaa ghoomanatatolana, andeh viheen ghoorna
 Then he went on the clean night of spring, on the backward road, he makes a tunnel of light from the headlight
 susheel berozegaar thisaliye shaayadzyada sochataa rahaa hoga is ghatnakram par
 3
 ujle din zaruraayenge, ujle din jarur aayengetank sareekhee bichhi hui har ore barfahai hawa kathin, haddi haddi ko thithuratiakash ugalta andhkaar phir ek barsanshay-videern aatma ram kii akulatihoga vah samar, abhi hoga kuch or bartab kahin megh ye chhin-bhinn ho paayenge
 Fat mice coming out of the cellars, spreading the smell of corpses, roaming, all the pictures of the mutilated ancestors, do not be afraid to roam around making fun of chickens, rats are the last rats, they will not be able to destroy the glory of life
 yah raktapaat, yah marpet jo machi huilogon ke dil bharamaa dene kaa zariyaa he
 The one who is adamant, scares us in the road, is a river of heavy fire
 sookhe chehre bacchon ke unki taral hanseeham yaad rakhenge, paar use kar jaayenge
 i do not give peace to lies
 There is a truth behind every dream, every time it ends, every difficulty gives some way
 aaye hai jab ham chalakar itane lakh varshaiske aage bhi tab chalakar hi jaayenge,aayenge, ujle din zarur aayenge
 4
 neendennind kii chhatariyaankai rangon or naap kii hai
 i like the sleep that descends from a strange light-hearted meadha, like a dry coconut falling from a tree, into a deserted one
 yaa phir vah neendjo gilahari kii tarah choti chanchal or foortili he
 Or it fits like a canop in the whole head
 ek or neend haikaheen samudri hawaaon ke ardra parade mempaldaar naav kaa mastul thameidhar ko daudi chali aatiiklautimsn adhed machherin

 paramparapahele usne hamaari smriti par danda barasaayeor kaha asal main yah tumhaari smriti haphir usne hamaare vivek kaa sunn kiyaor kaha ab jaakar hue tum vivekwanphir usne hamaari aankhon par pattee bandhior kaha chalo ab upanishad padhophir usne apni saji hui dongi hamaare rakt kinadi main utaar dior kaha ab apni to yahi he parampara

 The talk of toilet in Indian Railways is almost a hundred years old
 lekin aapako yah jaanakar hairaani hogi kibharat main pehali trainchalane ke pachaas saal baadatoilet kii jarurat mahasoos hui

 is patr ko1909main ek yatri ne likhaa tha
 Let me know what was it in that letter? In 1909, a passenger named Okhil Chandra Sen was traveling by passenger train
 us dauraan huabure anubhavon ko lekar unhone sahibganj rail divijan ke offis ko ek patr likhaa
 The letter was something like- "dear Shriman, i came to Ahmedpur station by a passenger train and i was swollen due to my stomach ache
 main shouch ke liye vahaan ekant main gaya

 main ekahath main lotaa or duusare haath main dhoti pakadakar dauda or tabhi platform par gir padaa

 meraa aapse vinamr nivedan heki janata kii bhalaai ke liye us guard par baari jurmaana karen

 wo in sabake liye apane coach vimal kumaar kaa bhi shukriya karte nahin thaktin
 She says that Vimal Kumar has worked hard with her in the last seven months and the result of all this is that she has again become World No
1
 ek shahar ke do super star
 
 
 Two such players whose dominance is not only in India but in the whole world
 duniya ke do world number 1 khilaadi or donon hyderabad se
 Both the games are different, the two world champions, who work on their respective courts on different grounds, have many things in common
 donon aaj kai megzine kii surkhiyon par chai hui hai
 Sponsor companies, fans and experts are willing to wager crores on them
 lekin is manzil tak pahunchane se pehle in donon ko mushkilon kaa pahaad paar karnaa padaa he
 Saina Nehwal says that it is not about Hyderabad
 baat india kii he
 The good thing is that it will not be impossible for many more young players to become World No
1
 sania bhi kuch aisi hi pratikriya de rahi hai
 She says that it is an amazing coincidence that both the world No
1 players are from the same city
 magar ye puure desh ke liye garv kii baat he or ab kai yuva khilaadi world number 1 banane kaa khwab dekh sakate hai
 Sania Mirza decided to quit playing singles about two years ago and started dreaming of becoming World No
1 in doubles
 is bich mahila dubles main unhen partner badalane kii zarurat bhi padi
 But Sania succumbed only after reaching the height
 sina kii kahani bhi kuch aisi hi he
 Like Sania, Saina is a role model for millions of youth
 sina pichley paanch saal se lagaataar top ten main rahete hue china kii mushkil diwaar ko todatii raheen or phir vahaan pahunch gayi jahaan pahunchane kaa khwab duniya kii kai khilaadiyon ne paal rakhaa he
 The comments donon ke world number 1 banane kii khushi hyderabad kii aam sadakon, skulon or maidaanon par mahasoos kii ja sakati he
 Many young players realize what these two players must have done to reach the top
 olympic padak vijeta sina nehwal or mixd dubles kii teen grand slam vijeta sania mirza ko vivaadon ke daur se bhi guzaranaa padaa he
 But proving every challenge to be small, these players have illuminated the name of Indian sports not only Hyderabad but also around the world

 sina nehwal kahati hai ki baat hyderabad kii nahin he
 The matter is about India
 acchhee baat ye he ki ab kai or yuva khilaadiyon ke liye world number 1 bananaa gairmumkin nahin lagegaa
 Sania is also giving a similar response
 wo kahati hai ki ye kamaal kaa ittifaaq he ki donon world number 1 khilaadi ek hi shahar se hai
 But it is a matter of pride for the whole country and now many young players can see the dream of becoming World No
1
 sania mirza ne qareeb do saal pehle singles khelnaa chhodane kaa faisalaa kiya or dubles main world number 1 banane kaa khwab paalane lageen
 Meanwhile, in women's doubles, she also had to change partner
 lekin sania ne bulandi par pahunchakar hi dam liya
 The story of Saina is also similar
 sania kii tarah hi sina bhi lakhon yuvaaon ke liye role model hai
 Saina has been in the top ten continuously for the last five years, breaking the difficult wall of China and then reached where many players of the world have pledged to reach
 tippaniyan The joy of both becoming World No
1 can be felt on the common roads, schools and grounds of Hyderabad
 kai yuva khilaadiyon ko is baat kaa ahsaas he ki in donon khilaadiyon ko top par pahunchane ke liye kya kuch karnaa padaa hoga
 Olympic medalist Saina Nehwal and three Grand Slam winners Sania Mirza of mixed doubles have also gone through a period of controversy
 lekin har chunauti ko chota sabit karti huin in khilaadiyon ne naa sirf hyderabad balki bhartiya khelon kaa naam duniya bhar main roshan kar diya he
 Sania is also giving a similar response
